"That can't be!" argued Jett, "It's just a flower plant."

"The 'flower' isn't a flower," Corbeau replied, "it's like a Poinsettia in that it has red leaves that only look like petals. That thing in the center that looks like the stamen is its trap, which it closes on its prey. The dew on the vines isn't dew either, it's a kind of glue-like nectar it uses to hang on to anything unfortunate enough to attract its attention."

"How big do they get?" asked Jett, her voice with a tinge of nervousness.

"Do you remember the plants I had at the gym? I heard shouting and witnessed one trying to attack a gym challenger's Lillipup." Corbeau said. "I mean this very seriously... I'm lucky Salazzle is part fire type, otherwise I don't know how we would have quelled the damned plant."

"Come to think of it," answered Jett, "the plant in my office was growing so fast it had to be repotted...Oh no! I left Tanzee in the office..." Suddenly realizing the mistake she'd made, Jett recalled her Clefable and ran to the elevator.

Corbeau followed her up to the penthouse floor where she had her office. Here she found the door, which she always left ajar, was closed.

Jett had to put pressure on the door, which creaked a protest as it opened, as if something was barricading it. She soon discovered what was responsible.

Somehow within the few hours she'd been away from the office, the entire room had been overtaken by vines. They stretched out from a singular point, the pot beside her desk, where the large blossom had closed its petals. From within their center the leaves were moving, shaking, as if the plant was struggling with something. Jett approached to get a closer look.

It was Tanzee. The plant had gotten ahold of the monkey and the animal was fighting it. Kicking it with all its might.

A horrified scream escaped her, and she leapt immediately towards the flower, having to tear aside the tendrils and leaves in an attempt to reach it. Tanzee for his part, gave it a deep bite and tore off some of the stem. The vines, as if possessed, lifted angrily in response, and she ended up fighting them back as it tries to trap as well.

At this point, Corbeau leapt in to help her. He opened a Poké Ball to send out his Salazzle.

"Salazzle, Flamethrower towards the vines," he ordered, and the lizard sent out a stream of fire. It struck the tendrils, which recoiled and withered immediately in the embers.

Jett grabbed Tanzee by the legs and yanked him loose of the carnivorous plant's grip. The plant was dead, but the small monkey was alive, and very angry. It started chattering loudly.

Corbeau took Jett by the arm and helped her out from the tangled, drooping vines. "Looks like Tanzee has lots to complain about," he remarked.

"Well..." said Jett giving her pet a hug, "actually he's yelling insults at the plant...some of it is saucy language...I'm guessing he picked it up from the gardening crew."

Jett smiled, and Corbeau smiled back at her and as she cradled the little monkey, he embraced her. "I'm glad you're both alright," he said.

"Marcus must've known something like this could happen," she realized, "He must've known the plant would get big enough at some point and attack me or Tanzee...or anyone who walks into my office, for that matter."

They were silent for a minute or so and the the phone rang, breaking their thoughts.

Corbeau glanced at the number displayed on the screen. "...It's Marcus. You should answer it."

There was a moment of hesitation before Jett let the monkey climb up to her shoulder and she snatched up the phone receiver. She held back her fury and said simply, "I'm busy. What do you want?"

Marcus noticed her curtness but chalked it up to being moody, so he replied in the same fashion. "Meet me at the top of Prism Tower."

Prism Tower. She turned her gaze out the window, towards the iconic building in the center of Lumiose.

The setting sun outlined the tower's gracefully arced column in shades of orange, the top part of which was now covered in flowering vines. Jett could scarcely believe the plants had spread outside of the rooftop garden so fast. Within a day or two they would probably overtake the entire structure.

She cursed the day she'd decided to entertain Marcus' plans without thinking things through, or ever thought there was a personal profit to be made in them. She'd been so shortsighted...so damned shortsighted.

"I'll be there," she replied.

She hung up the telephone, and glanced at Corbeau.

"He wants me to go to Prism Tower now."

"Jett, I don't trust this...I'll go and hide while you speak with him. You shouldn't be alone with him."

"That's up to you," she told him.

Jett walked around to the desk drawer and pulled out a small gun. She opened it, assured herself that it was loaded, and attached a silencer. Corbeau watched without expression, and simply recalled his Salazzle back into its Poké Ball.

"Let's go," she said, and they both walked out of the office.

Chapter 28 - Winter Caller ✅

The sunset had given way to nighttime in Lumiose City when Jett and Corbeau teleported up to the rooftop of Prism Tower with her Clefable. Up here at this hour it was desolate. Corbeau gave a brisk nod to Jett, and stepped soundlessly away to hide behind a wall within hearing distance.

The plants on the rooftop garden had grown gigantic. Some of the three-pronged red leaves with the center trap were easily eight feet high, and the vines draped themselves across anything they could. Jett was afraid to even get near them, but it was easy to steer clear of the vines. She recalled her Clefable and looked around for Marcus.

Observing the plants from a respectful distance, she found him.

"Lumiose City, the beautiful city of lights..." he contemplated, before she could speak, "It's those same lights that'll serve as a beacon to my army, so they know exactly where to target. I've left them orders to bombard the brightest city in Kalos."

"Marcus," said Jett simply, and she gestured towards the huge plants and the entanglement of vines that had seized Prism Tower, "Explain all this."

His eyebrows lifted almost jovially. "Now, you really didn't think I would take your claims at face value? I wouldn't launch an invasion of Lumiose or any other city without first ensuring victory."

She gazed at him, but not a word escaped her lips. He laughed and walked past her to the balcony.

"Success in warfare is partly psychological; if you succeed in demoralizing the enemy, it's easy to obliterate them," Marcus declared. "I'll soon have Lumiose City in terror over the plants. They'll be too fearful of the monsters growing in the ground to realize the attack coming from the sky. These flowers, you see, are my ultimate weapon."

"You lied to me," she said. Her voice was hoarse. "You didn't tell me they were carnivorous."

Marcus turned and faced Jett directly. "...and what of the fact you were dishonest? You claimed the mainland regions would be easy to take over. You omitted how large the rest of the world was."

"So neither of us was fully honest," Jett conceded. "What does it mean for Lumiose City?"

"I have decided to adjust my strategy. I don't need the rest of the world – quite yet. I'm perfectly content with the Kalos region. I should leave other regions unspoiled for my progeny to conquer and be acclaimed for in history, after all." He considered her briefly and went on, "I'm not one to overlook the many years of alliance your family has had with mine. You were of tremendous assistance with all the supply drops, not to mention you can still be the key to victory with your knowledge of this land."

"All I wanted was the south-eastern side of Lumiose razed," Jett said flatly.

"You've lamented countless times how petty bureaucracy prevents you from accomplishing what you want," Marcus said adding, "Do you think they will be any more forgiving, once they learn you had a hand in financing my army's little foray? Do you think the events in motion can be halted at this stage?"

He smirked knowingly when he saw her waver, and turned away pointedly to gaze out at the city's vast landscape.

"The only way to bypass those at the top is to be at the top. I'm going to wipe the slate as the new emperor," he added, "I'll abolish the city council and appoint you chief magistrate of Lumiose City under my reign...but only if you help."

"I intend to help." Her eyes narrowed. "With a clause."

"What's that?"

"I'm helping stop you."

He couldn't react to this before pain speared through his back, burning in a sudden explosion of fire. Marcus fell to the floor with an outcry, having only enough time to look up and see Jett holding a pistol with a silencer, the muzzle pointed level at his forehead.

"Survival of the fittest, darling," she smiled, and pulled the trigger.

Archer and Zoe were warped to a rooftop one block from Prism Tower. The moment Archer turned and saw the building, he had a double-take.

"Zoe, are you seeing this?"

The very top of Prism Tower and its spire was entwined with flowering vines in the manner of ivy. The plants seemed to originate from the rooftop garden.

The Unowns had apparently travelled there with them this time, and floated beside Archer, spelling out:

EVIL PLANTS

Archer took out binoculars and looked towards Prism Tower just in time to see Jett shoot Marcus and Corbeau come out of hiding.

"What is it Archer? What's happening?" Zoe asked.

"Jett just got rid of Marcus, and Corbeau is there so..." He turned to face the Unowns, "Guys, we need you to teleport us over there to Prism Tower."

The Unowns obliged immediately. Archer and Zoe found themselves warped away from them to the rooftop of Prism Tower within seconds.

Corbeau, having pocketed Faleris' Pal Sphere in his jacket, sent out Salazzle and ordered the lizard Pokémon to use its Flamethrower attack to incinerate Marcus' remains. Jett meanwhile stood with arms crossed, her eyes focused on the large plants to ensure they didn't move towards them.

Both Corbeau and Jett noticed Archer and Zoe standing off to the side, yet neither said anything, even as Corbeau recalled his Pokémon after having completed its grisly task. It was Archer who spoke first.

"Way to go, Corbeau!" Archer said, tactfully omitting what he'd witnessed through the binoculars, "You took care of the situation and saved us the trouble."

Jett spoke up. "I did it."

Zoe and Archer looked at each other, surprised she'd admit it. Zoe said, "Mrs. Silph, apparently we have underestimated you."

"I had no idea the plants were dangerous," Jett explained, "He kept that information from me, and the one plant I had in my office l attacked Tanzee...fortunately I arrived in time to save him..."

"No need to justify this to us, Jett," dismissed Archer, "We're Team Rocket, remember. The mission Giovanni sent us on was to eliminate Marcus... that son of a bitch had it coming to him."

"His army is guiding themselves by the city lights for their invasion," she explained. "Which, judging from the time, should be at any point now."

"In that case," considered Zoe, "the best thing to do is to throw the city into darkness. That way they won't know where to hit."

"The controls to all the city's electrical power are here at the top of Prism Tower. Corbeau is the one who knows exactly where..." Jett turned to face the gym leader, only to find him missing.

The little group suddenly sank into unease like if they'd stumbled into a mire. "Where's Corbeau?" asked Jett.

"He was just here a minute ago," said Archer.

Before anything more could be said, a large vine swept down and wrapped itself around Jett. She screamed but it tightened its grip even more. They now spied Corbeau in the middle of the entanglement, restrained by tendrils that had lassoed his wrists. Archer and Zoe ran to them and tried to loosen the vines but, just as an octopus had many tentacles, the plant had many vines and the others trapped Archer and Zoe as well.

Now, they were all at the mercy of the carnivorous plant. The gaping center trap inched closer and closer to them as they desperately sought a way to escape.

"That mouth is closer than it was a minute ago," observed Zoe.

Jett began writhing desperately, and Corbeau's attention shot towards her as the vines began to entwine themselves further around her torso.

"Stop moving!" snapped Corbeau, "It reacts when you move!"

She stopped struggling, yet she couldn't stop shivering. Jett stared at the giant plant, her eyes wide with fear.

Archer tensed. "Maybe if we can reach for a Poké Ball..."

"Wouldn't try it," whispered Corbeau, watching the blossom as its leaves seemed to quiver. "The moment you make a move for it, the plant will make a move for you."

For at least a full nerve-racking minute, they all stayed perfectly still, facing the towering predatory plant looming before them like a promise of death. As they watched, it visibly wavered, and slowly the giant 'flower' receded and its tendrils loosened its grasp on them.

The instant they were able to break free, both Archer and Corbeau sent out their Pokémon. Houndoom and Salazzle both emerged from their Poké Balls, ready for a fight.

"Houndoom, Inferno!" called Archer.

"Salazzle, use Flamethrower!" Corbeau ordered.

The flames engulfed the plant, which reeled back in the blaze. "Jett!" Corbeau called out to her, "The electricity switch!... It's located to the left side...pull it!"

Jett quickly sprang to the electrical panel and pulled the lever. The lights flickered only once, and Lumiose City was cast into a blackout.

"The city council will throw a fit," Jett observed.

"Yeah, and the regional government will breathe a sigh of relief once they realize we saved Lumiose," Archer replied, without missing a beat. "God willing that takes care of the invading army. Now we have to do something about the plants. They're all over the city. If the ones along the streets grow this big..."

"They can't be permitted to grow this big," Corbeau interjected. "We're going to need ten whole teams of Charizard to burn all of them."

"Or one strong frost," Jett said.

A thought occurred to Archer suddenly, and he turned towards Zoe.

"Zoe, you once said that Frostallion were revered on Palpagos Island for repelling calamities."

"Absolutely. I've heard the stories my whole life," she said, "they refer to them as the Winter Callers."

"I'm starting to think those alien stories might not have been so far off. Maybe around the era when Eternatus was attacking Galar, excess energy stretched to Palpagos Island like the tail of a hurricane and affected the plants there."

"That...sort of makes sense. Why else would they have been called 'Eternal' Flowers?" Zoe answered.

Archer had come up with a theory; a very crude theory, but still viable. All the strange phenomena that caused Pokémon to transform unnaturally – mega evolution from Kalos, dynamaxing from Galar – they all seemed to be different sides of the same coin, caused by the same type of energy that gave mainland Pokémon and island Pals the very ability to wield elements. Colress and the rest of the Pokémon professors would probably be able to say if that's a logical deduction... thought Archer, as he went on:

"Maybe Dryden's ancestors succeeded in getting some of the plants to germinate up on the Astral Mountains during wartime, and when people saw it they decided to surrender and flee the city there – without stopping to think the only reason they grew large in the past was a product of radiation," Archer guessed. "Then Marcus came along, realized that all the plants nowadays were small, then put two and two together and decided to try exposing them to the energy of Pokémon."

"That's all very interesting, but how does that help us with our present plight?" asked Jett.

"Well, if there were giant Eternal Flowers on Palpagos Island once upon a time, then the islanders must have found a way to eradicate them. Perhaps a Legendary Pal able to force a cold snap across the whole island."

He'd retrieved Frostallion's Poké Ball from his pocket, and opened the sphere in a flash of bright white light. The Pegasus emerged beside him, and reared up with a whinny.

"Frostallion..." Archer addressed it, "Zoe says your kind are nicknamed the Winter Callers on the island because you can summon blizzards. Is this true?"

Frostallion neighed affirmation, and jumped into the wind. Clouds gathered overhead, grey and vast and formless, and as the Pegasus looped around Prism Tower flying in widening concentric circles, ice billowed from its wings and the air began to grow incisive with cold.

"What a beautiful sight!" exclaimed Zoe.

"It's the middle of spring. People are going to be confused," commented Corbeau.

"I'm not confused, I'm just cold," Jett said flatly. "Hopefully this'll work."

Archer shrugged indifferently. "They'll probably figure a Legendary Pokémon did it. Which technically is true."

Archer looked up at the sky. Frostallion was basically waiting for his orders, so he complied.

"Frostallion! Use Crystal Breath over all the territory!"

The horse spread its wings and flew higher, stopping at some point to unleash a magnitude of ice power rarely seen. With just two blasts of frigid air, the entirety of Lumiose City was covered in ice and frost, and within seconds the monstrous plants began to die.

"It's working!" said Zoe, "Thanks to magnificent Frostallion!"

"Yes" agreed Archer, "now all we have to do is send out people to look for any stubborn plants that refuse to die and throw a fire type Pokémon at them."

"I can handle that," Corbeau interjected.

He was able to quickly contact his men from the Rust Syndicate and after explaining what was going on, gave a last order before sending them off. "...Burn the bastards!"

Archer recalled Frostallion, and then Jett teleported them all off to Corbeau's office.

By the following morning, all the Eternal Flowers were dead and everyone in Lumiose City was talking about it.

Archer turned to Corbeau and the two shook hands. "Nice battling with you...on the same side," smiled Archer.

"Same here," replied Corbeau, "When there's a mutual cause, an alliance is most beneficial."

"I'll be sure to mention it to Giovanni."

Corbeau nodded his head in response, and turned to Zoe. "I never did catch your full name, girl."

"It's Zoe Rayne," she replied extending her hand to shake his.

"You and I are distant cousins," Corbeau informed her, "My grandfather was one of the higher-ups in the Rayne Syndicate back in the day...and a cousin to Mr. Rayne, the boss. Grandfather fled to the Kalos region when the revolt happened on Palpagos Island. The plan was to have someone managing our offshore assets while the boss retook our tower base. Unfortunately it never came to be, and we lost contact with the island some years later. We slowly rebranded ourselves as the Rust Syndicate. At least, this was the family history that was passed down to me."

"Wow!" she exclaimed, "I never heard any of that. Thank you for telling me."

"Rayne Syndicate, Rust Syndicate. Rust may hide the vestiges of the past, but our business here on the mainland has stayed as strong as ever," added Corbeau with a proud smile.

"See you around, Corbeau," said Archer as he and Zoe turned to leave. It was then they noticed Jett. She was silently looking out the window at the cityscape. They approached her.

"Are you okay, Mrs. Silph?" Zoe asked.

Jett looked at her and said, "I'm alright. At least those that tried to hurt me and Tanzee are gone. Revenge is important to me."

"Totally agree, Jett," Archer replied. "Good luck."

He put his arm around Zoe and guided her away, and out of the building. When they got onto the sidewalk, the Unowns appeared with a trio of Team Rocket agents – Jessie, James, and Meowth.

"Hey! You guys are a sight for sore eyes!" Archer exclaimed happily.

"The boss is satisfied with your work, Archer," Meowth informed him, "He sent us to see if you and Zoe needed a ride back."

"That'll be fine," he replied, as the Unowns squeaked with joy.

"Well on the topic of Unowns..." Jessie said, "You know their cousins, the Zygarde?"

"Yeah."

"Apparently they didn't like the idea of their home here in Lumiose getting fucked with that way. They sought out Marcus' PIDF army out in the ocean. They got totally thrashed."

"The Zygarde?"

"No, the PIDF."

"Looks like all those Zygarde can combine into one giant Zygarde to kick ass," added James, "They sank all the islanders' ships and knocked out all their Pals in one swoop. I think it's fair to say that's the last we'll see of those well-laid plans of conquest."

"Good riddance!" said Zoe.

The crisis averted in Lumiose City, and Palpagos Island now completely ruled by Rocket Enterprises, life settled into a slower, more predictable pace for everyone. Giovanni gathered all the squadrons that were on the island, as well as the Syndicate members, for a meeting.

The information given out was basic. The Syndicate was no more, since all its members were now considered part of Team Rocket. Exceptions were given to those who wanted to get out of it and lead civilian lives. Team Rocket squadrons would rotate every two weeks on the island and go back to the mainland afterwards. Giovanni's intent was to ensure that no rogue group of islanders would rebel and grab hold of power. He would visit on occasion, but now he would return to the Kanto region along with his personal trio of guards, Jessie, James and Meowth.

At the moment what was first and foremost on Giovanni's mind was his wife Delia. He was eager to see her. He had been calling her every day he was on the island but a month had gone by and he missed the day-to-day life with her. They were both looking forward to reuniting.

As for Archer, he returned to the mainland. Zoe remained on the island as a coordinator of training for new recruits. They had parted ways amicably, and remained friends.

Thanks to Giovanni's investments, Palpagos Island was completely developed into an exotic resort for all on the mainland to visit. The island people benefited enormously from the tourism revenue, which only enhanced their loyalty towards Team Rocket and in particular towards Giovanni. Everyone on the island spoke highly of him, not by coercion but by admiration.

Yet despite all this, there was still something that remained an unaddressed curiosity to Archer. The tale he'd heard of Zygarde's power in defeating a whole army had left him with wonderment, and when the Unowns showed up again – as they tended to do, for no apparent reason, in the middle of Team Rocket headquarters in Celadon City to say hi and drift around Archer as if he was unofficially their trainer – he inquired:

"If your cousins have such power, what do you guys do?"

They looked at each other, and he elaborated:

"I mean, I know you teleport around and all that. But the few people who've been lucky enough to catch and train a single Unown say you guys know an attack called Hidden Power. No one has been able to figure out how it works. Do groups of Unown have another secret skill no human has seen yet?"

The Unown squeaked all at once in reply and twirled about in mid-air. One could have easily been forgiven for believing they were laughing – whether at the thought of such a notion or because they fully intended to keep their hidden power, hidden. And Archer could have also been forgiven for laughing right along with them.

Fin
